\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{chap10data3}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Died }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(chap10data3}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Died }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{, }\DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)}
\NormalTok{chap10data3.model1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{glm}\NormalTok{(Died }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ Birthweight, }\AttributeTok{family=}\FunctionTok{binomial}\NormalTok{(), }\AttributeTok{data=}\NormalTok{chap10data3)}
\FunctionTok{summary}\NormalTok{(chap10data3.model1)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\#diagnostic procedures

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]

\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
Influence measures of
     glm(formula = Died ~ Birthweight, family = binomial(), data = chap10data3) :

        dfb.1_  dfb.Brth     dffit cov.r   cook.d      hat inf
1     3.21e-03 -4.41e-03 -0.004907 1.001 1.59e-06 4.08e-04

\#fit logistic regression model

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]

                                               \AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"No"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{))}
\NormalTok{chap10data4.model1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{glm}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{as.factor}\NormalTok{(Died) }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ ., }\AttributeTok{family=}\FunctionTok{binomial}\NormalTok{(), }\AttributeTok{data=}\NormalTok{chap10data4)}

\#fit the final model

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{chap10data4.model2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{glm}\NormalTok{(Died }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ Delivery\_mode}\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{Birthweight}\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{Apgar\_score, }\AttributeTok{family=}\FunctionTok{binomial}\NormalTok{(), }\AttributeTok{data=}\NormalTok{chap10data4)}
\FunctionTok{summary}\NormalTok{(chap10data4.model2)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}

Call:
glm(formula = Died ~ Delivery_mode + Birthweight + Apgar_score, 
    family = binomial(), data = chap10data4)

Coefficients:
                       Estimate Std. Error z value Pr(>|z|)    
(Intercept)           1.1372630  0.3232827   3.518 0.000435 ***
Delivery_modeVaginal  0.9409230  0.2404518   3.913 9.11e-05 ***
Birthweight          -0.0014009  0.0001533  -9.138  < 2e-16 ***
Apgar_score          -0.3044104  0.0426201  -7.142 9.17e-13 ***
---
Signif. codes:  0 '***' 0.001 '**' 0.01 '*' 0.05 '.' 0.1 ' ' 1

(Dispersion parameter for binomial family taken to be 1)

    Null deviance: 926.40  on 2949  degrees of freedom
Residual deviance: 705.37  on 2946  degrees of freedom
AIC: 713.37

Number of Fisher Scoring iterations: 7
\end{verbatim}

\#Assess the final model

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Fit the logistic regression model}
\NormalTok{chap10data4.model2 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{glm}\NormalTok{(Died }\SpecialCharTok{\textasciitilde{}}\NormalTok{ Birthweight }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ Apgar\_score, }\AttributeTok{family =} \FunctionTok{binomial}\NormalTok{(), }\AttributeTok{data =}\NormalTok{ chap10data4)}

\CommentTok{\# Calculate predicted probabilities}
\NormalTok{chap10data4}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Probs }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{predict}\NormalTok{(chap10data4.model2, }\AttributeTok{type =} \StringTok{"response"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Generate predictions based on a threshold of 0.2}
\NormalTok{chap10data4}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Preds }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{ifelse}\NormalTok{(chap10data4}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Probs }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=} \FloatTok{0.2}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"No"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Convert predictions to a factor}
\NormalTok{chap10data4}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Preds }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{factor}\NormalTok{(chap10data4}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Preds, }\AttributeTok{levels =} \FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"No"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"Yes"}\NormalTok{))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}
